LEFT JOIN `public_users` AS `p` ON `m`.`public_user_id` = `p`.`Id`

LEFT JOIN `bot_styles` AS `b0` ON `b`.`style_id` = `b0`.`id`
WHERE `b`.`id` = @__id_0
ORDER BY `b`.`id`, `u`.`Id`, `b0`.`id`
LIMIT 1
